\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Initialize the device library for some resource application operations. \doxysubsection{函数说明}
\Hypertarget{GxIAPI_8h_a069f2cefb829d5b929259f1e85e05db3}\label{GxIAPI_8h_a069f2cefb829d5b929259f1e85e05db3} 
\index{GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}!GXCloseDevice@{GXCloseDevice}}
\index{GXCloseDevice@{GXCloseDevice}!GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXCloseDevice()}{GXCloseDevice()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXClose\+Device (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}}}]{h\+Device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Specify the device handle to close the device. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
Close the device handle that has been closed, return the GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE error. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The device handle that the user specified to close. The h\+Device can be get by GXOpen\+Device interface. \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE The illegal handle that the user introduces, or reclose the device. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


被这些函数引用 \mbox{\hyperlink{classGxCamera_af61afe2f0f130108e4bb50806cdd0d81}{Gx\+Camera\+::close()}}.

\Hypertarget{GxIAPI_8h_a6601fae30c60ad1da98e94ab478c1430}\label{GxIAPI_8h_a6601fae30c60ad1da98e94ab478c1430} 
\index{GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}!GXCloseLib@{GXCloseLib}}
\index{GXCloseLib@{GXCloseLib}!GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXCloseLib()}{GXCloseLib()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXClose\+Lib (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Close the device library to release resources. You must to call this interface to release resources when the Gx\+IAPI stopped all the controls of the device. Corresponding to the GXInit\+Lib. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


被这些函数引用 \mbox{\hyperlink{classGxCamera_af61afe2f0f130108e4bb50806cdd0d81}{Gx\+Camera\+::close()}} , 以及 \mbox{\hyperlink{classGxCamera_af2737ac031096690e6ee033171062725}{Gx\+Camera\+::open\+Device()}}.

\Hypertarget{GxIAPI_8h_afd8445d7a4164675bc832e33fa4ce8b4}\label{GxIAPI_8h_afd8445d7a4164675bc832e33fa4ce8b4} 
\index{GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}!GXDQAllBufs@{GXDQAllBufs}}
\index{GXDQAllBufs@{GXDQAllBufs}!GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXDQAllBufs()}{GXDQAllBufs()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXDQAll\+Bufs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}}}]{h\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a6e05811ef435cc7d0c8816593776984f}{PGX\+\_\+\+FRAME\+\_\+\+BUFFER}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pp\+Frame\+Buffer\+Array,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{n\+Frame\+Buffer\+Array\+Size,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pn\+Frame\+Count,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{n\+Time\+Out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



After starting the acquisition, all the buffers (zero copies) of the acquired images can be obtained through this interface. The order of the stored images in the image data array is from old to new, that is, pp\+Frame\+Buffer\+Array\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} stores the oldest image, and pp\+Frame\+Buffer\+Array\mbox{[}n\+Frame\+Count -\/ 1\mbox{]} stores the latest image. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The handle of the device. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Array of image data pointers. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The number of applications for image arrays. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Returns the number of actual filled images. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Take timeout time (unit\+: ms). \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE The handle that the user introduces is illegal. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+PARAMETER The pointer that the user introduces is NULL. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CALL Acquisition is not started or the callback is registered. It is not allowed to call the interface. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NEED\+\_\+\+MORE\+\_\+\+BUFFER Insufficient buffer requested by the user\+: When reading,the user input buffer size is smaller than the actual need. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+TIMEOUT Acquire image timeout error. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+ERROR Unspecified internal errors that are not expected to occur. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{GxIAPI_8h_a4fc397772b16f506da27bf484b4db5c2}\label{GxIAPI_8h_a4fc397772b16f506da27bf484b4db5c2} 
\index{GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}!GXDQBuf@{GXDQBuf}}
\index{GXDQBuf@{GXDQBuf}!GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXDQBuf()}{GXDQBuf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXDQBuf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}}}]{h\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a6e05811ef435cc7d0c8816593776984f}{PGX\+\_\+\+FRAME\+\_\+\+BUFFER}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pp\+Frame\+Buffer,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{n\+Time\+Out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



After starting the acquisition, an image (zero copy) can be acquired through this interface. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The handle of the device. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Address pointer of image data output by the interface. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Take timeout time (unit\+: ms). \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE The handle that the user introduces is illegal. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+PARAMETER The pointer that the user introduces is NULL. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CALL Acquisition is not started or the callback is registered. It is not allowed to call the interface. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+TIMEOUT Acquire image timeout error. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+ERROR Unspecified internal errors that are not expected to occur. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}!GXFlushEvent@{GXFlushEvent}}
\index{GXFlushEvent@{GXFlushEvent}!GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXFlushEvent()}{GXFlushEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXFlush\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}}}]{h\+Device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Empty the device event, such as the frame exposure to end the event data queue. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
The library internal event data receiving and processing using caching mechanism, if the user receiving, processing event speed is slower than the event generates, then the event data will be accumulated in the library, it will affect the the user to get real-\/time event data. If you want to get the real-\/time event data, you need to call the GXFlush\+Event interface to clear the event cache data. This interface empties all the event data at once. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The handle of the device. \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE The handle that the user introduces is illegal. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{GxIAPI_8h_a0c6ab3461f62473e8d19029fa649f9bb}\label{GxIAPI_8h_a0c6ab3461f62473e8d19029fa649f9bb}

\index{GXFlushQueue@{GXFlushQueue}!GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXFlushQueue()}{GXFlushQueue()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXFlush\+Queue (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}}}]{h\+Device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Empty the cache image in the image output queue. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
If the user processes the images too slow, the image of last acquisition may be remained in the queue. Especially in the trigger mode, after the user send the trigger signal, and get the old image (last image). If you want to get the current image that corresponding to trigger signal, you should call the GXFlush\+Queue interface before sending the trigger signal to empty the image output queue. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\

GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE The handle that the user introduces is illegal. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST.

\Hypertarget{GxIAPI_8h_ab8eaebce532e2beceb41100202b0a873}\label{GxIAPI_8h_ab8eaebce532e2beceb41100202b0a873} 
\index{GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}!GXGetImage@{GXGetImage}}
\index{GXGetImage@{GXGetImage}!GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXGetImage()}{GXGetImage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXGet\+Image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}}}]{h\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structGX__FRAME__DATA}{GX\+\_\+\+FRAME\+\_\+\+DATA}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Frame\+Data,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{n\+Timeout }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



After starting acquisition, you can call this function to get images directly. Noting that the interface can not be mixed with the callback capture mode. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
The GXGet\+Image interface is not allowed to be called after the capture callback function is registered, and the call will return GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CALL error. When using high resolution cameras for high-\/speed acquisition, because there is a buffer copy within the GXGet\+Image interface, it will affect the transport performance. It is recommended that users use the capture callback mode in this case. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The handle of the device. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The pointer to the address that the user introduced to receive the image data. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The timeout time of capture image (unit\+: ms). \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE The handle that the user introduces is illegal. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CALL After registering the capture callback function, the user calls the GXGet\+Image to get image. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+PARAMETER User incoming image address pointer is NULL. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NEED\+\_\+\+MORE\+\_\+\+BUFFER Insufficient buffer requested by the user\+: When reading,the user input buffer size is smaller than the actual need. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{GxIAPI_8h_a56c5274c527611754b0c3e52b58da0c0}\label{GxIAPI_8h_a56c5274c527611754b0c3e52b58da0c0}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXGet\+String\+Max\+Length (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}}}]{h\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8ba4fbf8984c27bb5f34c26274d0bdfc}{GX\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+ID\+\_\+\+CMD}}}]{feature\+ID,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pn\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the maximum length of the string type value. Unit\+: byte. The user allocates buffer according to the length information obtained, then call the GXGet\+String to get the string information. This interface can get the maximum possible length of the string (including the terminator \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{} 0\textquotesingle{}), but the actual length of the string might not be that long, if the user wants to allocate buffer according to the actual string length, the user can call the GXGet\+String\+Length interface to get the actual string length.

\Hypertarget{GxIAPI_8h_a221acff1913d90f6649436bd74f403bc}\label{GxIAPI_8h_a221acff1913d90f6649436bd74f403bc} 
\index{GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}!GXInitLib@{GXInitLib}}
\index{GXInitLib@{GXInitLib}!GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXInitLib()}{GXInitLib()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXInit\+Lib (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initialize the device library for some resource application operations. This interface must be called before using the Gx\+IAPI to interact with the camera, and the GXClose\+Lib must be called to release all the resources when the Gx\+IAPI is stopped for all control of the device. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
Before calling the other interfaces (except GXClose\+Lib/ GXGet\+Last\+Error), you must call the GXInit\+Lib interface for initialization first, otherwise the error GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API will return. 
\end{DoxyAttention}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful, no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+FOUND\+\_\+\+TL Can not found the library. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


被这些函数引用 \mbox{\hyperlink{classGxCamera_a6f5af3c930b1b0c5e6304bfaf1a799e4}{Gx\+Camera\+::initial()}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXIs\+Implemented (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}}}]{h\+Device,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8ba4fbf8984c27bb5f34c26274d0bdfc}{GX\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+ID\+\_\+\+CMD}}}]{feature\+ID,  }\item[{bool \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pb\+Is\+Implemented }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Inquire the current camera whether support a special feature. Usually the camera does not support a feature means that\+: 1) By inquiring the camera register, the current camera really does not support this feature. 2) There is no description of this feature in the current camera description file. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The handle of the device. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The feature code ID. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
To return the result whether is support this feature. If support, then returns true, if not support, false will return. \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE The handle that the user introduces is illegal. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+PARAMETER The pointer that the user input is NULL. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


被这些函数引用 \mbox{\hyperlink{classGxCamera_af2737ac031096690e6ee033171062725}{Gx\+Camera\+::open\+Device()}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXOpen\+Device (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structGX__OPEN__PARAM}{GX\+\_\+\+OPEN\+\_\+\+PARAM}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Open\+Param,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Open the device by a specific unique identification, such as\+: SN, IP, MAC, Index etc. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
It is recommended that you call the Gx\+Update\+Device\+List() interface to make an enumeration before calling the function. To ensure that device list within the library is consistent with the current device. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The open device parameter which is configurated by user. Ref\+:\doxylink{structGX__OPEN__PARAM}{GX\+\_\+\+OPEN\+\_\+\+PARAM}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The device handle returned by the interface. \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+PARAMETER The pointer that the user input is NULL. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+FOUND\+\_\+\+DEVICE Not found the device that matches the specific information. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+ACCESS The device can not be opened under the current access mode. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The feature code ID. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The handle of property update callback function, to unregister the callback function. \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE The handle that the user introduces is illegal. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+PARAMETER The unsupported event ID or the callback function is illegal. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParams}

\index{GXUnregisterCaptureCallback@{GXUnregisterCaptureCallback}!GxIAPI.h@{GxIAPI.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXUnregisterCaptureCallback()}{GXUnregisterCaptureCallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXUnregister\+Capture\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_a8e9793aaf704936a037db9c3548a096a}{GX\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HANDLE}}}]{h\+Device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Unregister the capture callback function, corresponding to GXRegister\+Capture\+Callback. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
Before sending the stop acquisition command, the user can not unregister the callback function. Otherwise, it will return GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CALL. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The handle of the device. \begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+HANDLE The handle that the user introduces is illegal. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CALL After sending the stop acquisition command, the user can not unregister the capture callback function. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GXUpdateAllDeviceList()}{GXUpdateAllDeviceList()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{GxIAPI_8h_ad02930e4573c489f8c5703aaf4d3425b}{GX\+\_\+\+API}} GXUpdate\+All\+Device\+List (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pun\+Num\+Devices,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{n\+Time\+Out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enumerating currently all available devices in entire network and gets the number of devices. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em pun\+Num\+Devices} & The address pointer used to return the number of devices, and the pointer can not be NULL. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em un\+Time\+Out} & The timeout time of enumeration (unit\+: ms). If the device is successfully enumerated within the specified timeout time, the value returns immediately. If the device is not enumerated within the specified timeout time, then it waits until the specified timeout time is over and then it returns. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS The operation is successful and no error occurs. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INIT\+\_\+\+API The GXInit\+Lib initialization library is not called. GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+PARAMETER The pointer that the user input is NULL. The errors that are not covered above please reference GX\+\_\+\+STATUS\+\_\+\+LIST. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
